[Wed Apr  1 00:28:32 2020] INF: [ubomaterial.cpp (54)] UBO Material creado
[Wed Apr  1 00:28:32 2020] INF: [shader.cpp (169)] Compilando ../p6a/gouraud.vert
[Wed Apr  1 00:28:32 2020] ERR: [program.cpp (223)] Error compilando el shader:0(76) : error C0000: syntax error, unexpected reserved word "float", expecting ',' or ';' at token "float"
0(84) : error C1020: invalid operands to "<"
0(90) : error C1115: unable to find compatible overloaded function "pow(vec3, float)"
0(93) : error C1503: undefined variable "factorAtenuacion"

Vertex shader: ../p6a/gouraud.vert
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |
 49 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 50 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 51 |
 52 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 53 |
 54 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 55 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 56 |      continue;
 57 |
 58 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 59 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |
 64 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 65 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 66 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 67 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 68 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 69 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 70 |    }
 71 |    
 72 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 73 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos)
 74 |
 75 |    // Factor atenuacin
 76 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 77 |
 78 |    // Efecto foco
 79 |    float efectoFoco;
 80 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 81 |    {
 82 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 83 |    }
 84 |    else if (max(-L*lights[i].spotDirectionWorld, 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice dentro del cono iluminado
 85 |    { 
 86 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 87 |    }
 88 |    else
 89 |    {
 90 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(-L*lights[i].spotDirectionWorld, 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 91 |    }
 92 |
 93 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 94 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
 97 |
 98 |  }
 99 |
100 |  return color;
101 |}
102 |
103 |void main() {
104 |
105 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
107 |
108 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
109 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
110 |
111 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
112 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
113 |
114 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
115 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
116 |
117 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
118 |}
119 |

Vertex shader: ../p6a/gouraud.vert
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |
 49 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 50 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 51 |
 52 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 53 |
 54 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 55 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 56 |      continue;
 57 |
 58 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 59 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |
 64 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 65 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 66 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 67 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 68 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 69 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 70 |    }
 71 |    
 72 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 73 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos)
 74 |
 75 |    // Factor atenuacin
 76 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 77 |
 78 |    // Efecto foco
 79 |    float efectoFoco;
 80 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 81 |    {
 82 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 83 |    }
 84 |    else if (max(-L*lights[i].spotDirectionWorld, 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice dentro del cono iluminado
 85 |    { 
 86 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 87 |    }
 88 |    else
 89 |    {
 90 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(-L*lights[i].spotDirectionWorld, 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 91 |    }
 92 |
 93 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 94 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
 97 |
 98 |  }
 99 |
100 |  return color;
101 |}
102 |
103 |void main() {
104 |
105 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
107 |
108 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
109 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
110 |
111 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
112 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
113 |
114 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
115 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
116 |
117 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
118 |}
119 |

Vertex shader: ../p6a/gouraud.vert
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |
 49 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 50 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 51 |
 52 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 53 |
 54 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 55 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 56 |      continue;
 57 |
 58 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 59 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |
 64 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 65 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 66 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 67 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 68 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 69 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 70 |    }
 71 |    
 72 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 73 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos)
 74 |
 75 |    // Factor atenuacin
 76 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 77 |
 78 |    // Efecto foco
 79 |    float efectoFoco;
 80 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 81 |    {
 82 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 83 |    }
 84 |    //else if (max(-L*lights[i].spotDirectionWorld, 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice dentro del cono iluminado
 85 |    //{ 
 86 |    //    efectoFoco = 0;
 87 |    //}
 88 |    else
 89 |    {
 90 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 91 |    }
 92 |
 93 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 94 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
 97 |
 98 |  }
 99 |
100 |  return color;
101 |}
102 |
103 |void main() {
104 |
105 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
107 |
108 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
109 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
110 |
111 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
112 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
113 |
114 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
115 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
116 |
117 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
118 |}
119 |

Vertex shader: ../p6a/gouraud.vert
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |
 49 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 50 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 51 |
 52 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 53 |
 54 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 55 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 56 |      continue;
 57 |
 58 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 59 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |
 64 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 65 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 66 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 67 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 68 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 69 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 70 |    }
 71 |    
 72 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 73 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 74 |
 75 |    // Factor atenuacin
 76 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 77 |
 78 |    // Efecto foco
 79 |    float efectoFoco;
 80 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 81 |    {
 82 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 83 |    }
 84 |    else if (max(-L*lights[i].spotDirectionWorld, 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice dentro del cono iluminado
 85 |    { 
 86 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 87 |    }
 88 |    else
 89 |    {
 90 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 91 |    }
 92 |
 93 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 94 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
 97 |
 98 |  }
 99 |
100 |  return color;
101 |}
102 |
103 |void main() {
104 |
105 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
107 |
108 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
109 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
110 |
111 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
112 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
113 |
114 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
115 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
116 |
117 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
118 |}
119 |

Vertex shader: ../p6a/gouraud.vert
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 47 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 48 |
 49 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 50 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 51 |
 52 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 53 |
 54 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 55 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 56 |      continue;
 57 |
 58 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 59 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 60 |
 61 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 62 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 63 |
 64 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 65 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 66 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 67 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 68 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 69 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 70 |    }
 71 |    
 72 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 73 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 74 |
 75 |    // Factor atenuacin
 76 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 77 |
 78 |    // Efecto foco
 79 |    float efectoFoco;
 80 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 81 |    {
 82 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 83 |    }
 84 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice fuera del cono iluminado
 85 |    { 
 86 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 87 |    }
 88 |    else
 89 |    {
 90 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotCosCutoff), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 91 |    }
 92 |
 93 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 94 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 95 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 96 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
 97 |
 98 |  }
 99 |
100 |  return color;
101 |}
102 |
103 |void main() {
104 |
105 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
106 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
107 |
108 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
109 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
110 |
111 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
112 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
113 |
114 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
115 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
116 |
117 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
118 |}
119 |

Vertex shader: ../p6b/gouraud.vert
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |
 46 |out vec3 N;
 47 |out vec3 L[];
 48 |
 49 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 50 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 51 |
 52 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 53 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 54 |
 55 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 56 |
 57 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 58 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 59 |      continue;
 60 |
 61 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 62 |    L[i] = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 63 |
 64 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 65 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 66 |
 67 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 68 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 69 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 70 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L[i], N);
 71 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 72 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 73 |    }
 74 |    
 75 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 76 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 77 |
 78 |    // Factor atenuacin
 79 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 80 |
 81 |    // Efecto foco
 82 |    float efectoFoco;
 83 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 84 |    {
 85 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 86 |    }
 87 |    else if (max(dot(-L[i],lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice fuera del cono iluminado
 88 |    { 
 89 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 90 |    }
 91 |    else
 92 |    {
 93 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L[i],lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 94 |    }
 95 |
 96 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 97 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 98 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
 99 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
100 |
101 |  }
102 |
103 |  return color;
104 |}
105 |
106 |void main() {
107 |
108 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
109 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
110 |
111 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
112 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
113 |
114 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
115 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
116 |
117 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
118 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
119 |
120 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
121 |}
122 |

 93 |    else
 94 |    {
 95 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 96 |    }
 97 |
 98 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 99 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
100 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
101 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
102 |
103 |  }
104 |
105 |  return color;
106 |}
107 |
108 |void main() {
109 |  color = iluminacion(eposition, Nfrag, Vfrag);
110 |  fragColor = color;
111 |}

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 color;
 42 |in vec3 fragPos;
 43 |in vec3 fragN;
 44 |in vec3 fragL[];
 45 |in vec3 fragV;
 46 |
 47 |
 48 |out vec4 fragColor;
 49 |
 50 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 51 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 52 |
 53 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 54 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 55 |
 56 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 57 |
 58 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 59 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 60 |      continue;
 61 |
 62 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 63 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 64 |
 65 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 66 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 67 |
 68 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 69 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 70 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 71 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 72 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 73 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 74 |    }
 75 |    
 76 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 77 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 78 |
 79 |    // Factor atenuacin
 80 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 81 |
 82 |    // Efecto foco
 83 |    float efectoFoco;
 84 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 85 |    {
 86 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 87 |    }
 88 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice fuera del cono iluminado
 89 |    { 
 90 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 91 |    }
 92 |    else
 93 |    {
 94 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 95 |    }
 96 |
 97 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 98 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
 99 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
100 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
101 |
102 |  }
103 |
104 |  return color;
105 |}
106 |
107 |void main() {
108 |  color = iluminacion(fragPos, fragN, fragV);
109 |  fragColor = color;
110 |}
111 |

Vertex shader: ../p6b/gouraud.vert
----------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |out vec3 fragPos;
 46 |out vec3 fragN;
 47 |out vec3 fragL[];
 48 |out vec3 fragV;
 49 |
 50 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 51 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 52 |
 53 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 54 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 55 |
 56 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 57 |
 58 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 59 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 60 |      continue;
 61 |
 62 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 63 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 64 |    fragL[i] = L;
 65 |
 66 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 67 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 68 |
 69 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 70 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 71 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 72 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 73 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 74 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 75 |    }
 76 |    
 77 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 78 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 79 |
 80 |    // Factor atenuacin
 81 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 82 |
 83 |    // Efecto foco
 84 |    float efectoFoco;
 85 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 86 |    {
 87 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 88 |    }
 89 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice fuera del cono iluminado
 90 |    { 
 91 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 92 |    }
 93 |    else
 94 |    {
 95 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 96 |    }
 97 |
 98 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 99 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
100 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
101 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
102 |
103 |  }
104 |
105 |  return color;
106 |}
107 |
108 |void main() {
109 |
110 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
111 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
112 |  fragN = eN;
113 |
114 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
115 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
116 |  fragPos = eposition;
117 |
118 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
119 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
120 |  fragV = V;
121 |
122 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
123 |  //color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
124 |  color = vec4(0, 0, 0, 0);
125 |
126 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
127 |}

  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 position;
 42 |in vec3 normal;
 43 |
 44 |out vec4 color;
 45 |out vec3 fragPos;
 46 |out vec3 fragN;
 47 |out vec3 fragL[4];
 48 |out vec3 fragV;
 49 |
 50 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 51 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 V) {
 52 |
 53 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 54 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 55 |
 56 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 57 |
 58 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 59 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 60 |      continue;
 61 |
 62 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 63 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 64 |    fragL[i] = L;
 65 |
 66 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 67 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 68 |
 69 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 70 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 71 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 72 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 73 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 74 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 75 |    }
 76 |    
 77 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 78 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 79 |
 80 |    // Factor atenuacin
 81 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 82 |
 83 |    // Efecto foco
 84 |    float efectoFoco;
 85 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 86 |    {
 87 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 88 |    }
 89 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice fuera del cono iluminado
 90 |    { 
 91 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 92 |    }
 93 |    else
 94 |    {
 95 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 96 |    }
 97 |
 98 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 99 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
100 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
101 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
102 |
103 |  }
104 |
105 |  return color;
106 |}
107 |
108 |void main() {
109 |
110 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
111 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
112 |  fragN = eN;
113 |
114 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
115 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
116 |  fragPos = eposition;
117 |
118 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
119 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
120 |  fragV = V;
121 |
122 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
123 |  //color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
124 |  color = vec4(0, 0, 0, 0);
125 |
126 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
127 |}

Fragment shader: ../p6b/gouraud.frag
------------------------------------
  1 |#version 420
  2 |
  3 |layout (std140, binding=0) uniform GLMatrices {
  4 |  mat4 modelMatrix;
  5 |  mat4 viewMatrix;
  6 |  mat4 projMatrix;
  7 |  mat4 modelviewMatrix;
  8 |  mat4 modelviewprojMatrix;
  9 |  mat3 normalMatrix;
 10 |};
 11 |struct LightSource {
 12 |  vec4 ambient, diffuse, specular;
 13 |  vec4 positionWorld;
 14 |  vec4 positionEye;
 15 |  vec3 spotDirectionWorld;
 16 |  int directional;
 17 |  vec3 spotDirectionEye;
 18 |  int enabled;
 19 |  float spotExponent, spotCutoff, spotCosCutoff;
 20 |  vec3 attenuation;
 21 |};
 22 |layout (std140, binding=2) uniform Lights {
 23 |  LightSource lights[4];
 24 |};
 25 |layout (std140, binding=1) uniform Material {
 26 |vec4 diffuse;
 27 |vec4 ambient;
 28 |vec4 specular;
 29 |vec4 emissive;
 30 |float shininess;
 31 |int textureCount;
 32 |};
 33 |
 34 |uint numDiffTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 0, 3); }
 35 |uint numSpecTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 3, 3); }
 36 |uint numNormTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 6, 3); }
 37 |uint numHeightTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 9, 3); }
 38 |uint numOpacTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 12, 3); }
 39 |uint numAmbTextures() { return bitfieldExtract(textureCount, 15, 3); }
 40 |
 41 |in vec4 color;
 42 |in vec3 fragPos;
 43 |in vec3 fragN;
 44 |in vec3 fragL[4];
 45 |in vec3 fragV;
 46 |
 47 |
 48 |out vec4 fragColor;
 49 |
 50 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales
 51 |vec4 iluminacion(vec3 pos, vec3 N, vec3 fragL[], vec3 V) {
 52 |
 53 |  // Componente emisiva del material
 54 |  vec4 color = emissive;
 55 |
 56 |  for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
 57 |
 58 |    // Si la fuente est apagada, no tenerla en cuenta
 59 |    if (lights[i].enabled == 0)
 60 |      continue;
 61 |
 62 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 63 |    //vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 64 |    vec3 L = normalize(fragL[i]);
 65 |
 66 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 67 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 68 |
 69 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 70 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 71 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 72 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 73 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 74 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 75 |    }
 76 |    
 77 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 78 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 79 |
 80 |    // Factor atenuacin
 81 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 82 |
 83 |    // Efecto foco
 84 |    float efectoFoco;
 85 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 86 |    {
 87 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 88 |    }
 89 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice fuera del cono iluminado
 90 |    { 
 91 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 92 |    }
 93 |    else
 94 |    {
 95 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionWorld), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 96 |    }
 97 |
 98 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 99 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
100 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
101 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
102 |
103 |  }
104 |
105 |  return color;
106 |}
107 |
108 |void main() {
109 |  fragColor = iluminacion(fragPos, fragN, fragL, fragV);
110 |  //fragColor = color;
111 |}
112 |

 51 |// Suponiendo fuentes puntuales

 61 |      continue;
 62 |
 63 |    // Vector iluminacin (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 64 |    vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - pos);
 65 |
 66 |    // Multiplicador de la componente difusa
 67 |    float diffuseMult = max(dot(N, L), 0.0);
 68 |
 69 |    float specularMult = 0.0;
 70 |    if (diffuseMult > 0.0) {
 71 |      // Multiplicador de la componente especular
 72 |      vec3 R = reflect(-L, N);
 73 |      specularMult = max(0.0, dot(R, V));
 74 |      specularMult = pow(specularMult, shininess);
 75 |    }
 76 |    
 77 |    // Distancia (desde vrtice a la fuente)
 78 |    float d = distance(vec3(lights[i].positionEye), pos);
 79 |
 80 |    // Factor atenuacin
 81 |    float factorAtenuacion = 1 / max(1, lights[i].attenuation[0] + lights[i].attenuation[1] * d + lights[i].attenuation[2] * d * d);
 82 |
 83 |    // Efecto foco
 84 |    float efectoFoco;
 85 |    if (lights[i].spotCutoff == 180) // La fuente no es focal
 86 |    {
 87 |        efectoFoco = 1;
 88 |    }
 89 |    else if (max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0) < lights[i].spotCosCutoff) // Vrtice fuera del cono iluminado
 90 |    { 
 91 |        efectoFoco = 0;
 92 |    }
 93 |    else
 94 |    {
 95 |        efectoFoco = pow(max(dot(-L,lights[i].spotDirectionEye), 0), lights[i].spotExponent);
 96 |    }
 97 |
 98 |    color += factorAtenuacion * efectoFoco *
 99 |             ( lights[i].ambient * ambient +
100 |               lights[i].diffuse * diffuse * diffuseMult +
101 |               lights[i].specular * specular * specularMult );
102 |
103 |  }
104 |
105 |  return color;
106 |}
107 |
108 |void main() {
109 |
110 |  // Normal en el espacio de la cmara
111 |  vec3 eN = normalize(normalMatrix * normal);
112 |  fragN = eN;
113 |
114 |  // Vrtice en el espacio de la cmara
115 |  vec3 eposition = vec3(modelviewMatrix * position);
116 |  fragPos = eposition;
117 |
118 |  // Vector vista (desde vrtice a la cmara)
119 |  vec3 V = normalize(-eposition.xyz);
120 |  fragV = V;
121 |
122 |  // Clculo de la iluminacin
123 |  if(phong) {  // Por fragmento
124 |    for (int i = 0; i < lights.length(); i++) {
125 |      vec3 L = normalize(vec3(lights[i].positionEye) - eposition);
126 |      fragL[i] = L;
127 |    }
128 |  } else { // Por vrtice
129 |    color = iluminacion(eposition, eN, V);
130 |  }
131 |
132 |  gl_Position = modelviewprojMatrix * position;
133 |}
134 |
